< Review>
I absolutely love the cupcakes here.  I never used to eat cupcake since they tend to lack flavor, texture and most of the time too sweet.  These cupcakes are the best I ever had.  I found them because I was looking to have cupcakes for my wedding base on wedding planning reviews of using cupcakes instead of a traditional cake.

I tasted many before I decided on Love at First Bite and I have to tell you it was a "Big Hit" at my wedding.  Everyone still talk about the great cupcakes to this day.

I love the mud pie and the red velvet best and so did my husband.  For the bride and groom cupcakes I chose the red velvet and he chose mud pie.  It was just so beautiful.

Their service was great.  We got the cupcakes at the time we wanted delivered. They do offer cupcake set up for an additional charge but my friend volunteered to display them. Everything turned beautifully! If you haven't try their cupcakes I highly suggest you give it a chance.<//Review>

< Review>
Tucked in an alley around the corner from the original Peet's Coffee, you'll find Love at First Bite. I've worked with them on a few weddings and I ordered from them for my birthday in April. Definitely the red velvet and cookies and cream are guaranteed to make your mouth dance in delight! The green tea cupcake and pistachio cupcakes are on the novel side of the spectrum and are good but if you are ordering for a party the first two are sure to be the most popular. The prices are average, about $3-3.50 for a full size cupcake. You can pick up cute party supplies, confections and toppers here too.< /Review>

<Name>Russell Wolfkiel</Name><time>1503441291539<//time><rating>5</rating>< Text>
Five stars for value and flexibility. If you're looking for elegant dining, look somewhere else but if you are looking for the best breakfast value in "the city in the country," this is the place to go.

The staff is very warm and friendly. Don't feel constrained by the written menu options, if you want to substitute pancakes for your toast they will let you do it. Don't forget refried beans are available to be substituted for the hashbrowns or kountry potato option and for just a dollar more you could have french fries with your breakfast instead.

The portions are American sized so bring your appetite. I highly recommend the breakfast quesadilla, it will fill your entire plate and even the hungriest tummy. My wife would advise to get the hash-brown tower or to go off script by customizing any of the menu options to your liking.

Help me out by asking them to bring back the Chili Verde Omelette; it was the best thing on the menu and I want the chance to eat it again!< /Text>

<rate>3<//rate>< Review>
Walking in head first, it had a great and fresh atmosphere. As my husband and I approached the register, we were greeted by a sweet woman. She was informative and would even suggest options that weren't on the new menu. It was our first time here and everything sounded great the way it was pitched to us.

So we both decided to order a few items, which ended up being the Tenders & Fries ($5.99), 13" Medium Deluxe Calzone ($17.99), 8 Piece Boneless Chicken Wings BBQ style ($9.99) ... and to top it off with a Mexican Coke ($2.49) seemed a bit pricey, but I decided to pay the price considering how big the cashier made the order sound.

Once we got our food to go, the packaging was cute, secured, and high quality as it didn't seem like anything would be spilling or filled with grease.

Heading home, we decided to try the Chicken Tenders & Fries first, which ... was a little disappointing to say the least. The portion came with only three medium sized chicken tenders and a pretty small batch of unsalted steak fries. The Deluxe Calzone was much smaller than anticipated, and the boneless wings were saltier than I'd imagine.

If you're looking for an authentic Italian Pizzeria, this might be the place for you. Though, not the best place if your looking for quantity and a good deal on prices.</Review>

(Translated by Google) POPULAR PIZZERIA IN LOS ANGELES

Big Mama's & Papa's Pizzeria is a popular pizzeria that has more than 10 locations in Los Angeles. They are best known for their huge pizzas, which we did not get to try this time around.

We were past the department at Hollywood Bvld. in Little Armenia just across the border from Hollywood, where we chose to build our own pizza.

The decor is nice and the service is okay while the prices are moderate.

We paid 13 USD for a medium pizza, which is equivalent to 80 DKK.

Big Mama's & Papa's Pizzeria is a mediocre pizzeria, which is generally acceptable, but in terms of price we expect much more taste.
